		<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
	var ad_hide_by_width_n = true;
	var ad_hide_by_width = true;
	var ad_showed_from_n = {};
	var ad_page_keywords_n = new Object([]);
	var ad_page_keywords_str_n =(ad_page_keywords_n.length>0) ? ad_page_keywords_n.join(";")+";" : "";
	var ad_page_keywords_str_n_space =(ad_page_keywords_n.length>0) ? ad_page_keywords_n.join(" ")+" " : "";
	var ad_local_contents_n = new Object({"contents":[],"templates":[]});

	var ad_geo_ip_country_n = String(getCookie("geo_ip_country"));
	if(ad_geo_ip_country_n.length !== 2 ){
		ad_geo_ip_country_n = "A0";
	}
	var ad_geo_ip_city_id_n = parseInt(getCookie("geo_ip_city_id"));
	if(ad_geo_ip_city_id_n < 0 ){
		ad_geo_ip_city_id_n = 0;
	}
	var ad_geo_ip_oblast_id_n = parseInt(getCookie("geo_ip_oblast_id"));
	if(ad_geo_ip_oblast_id_n < 0 ){
		ad_geo_ip_oblast_id_n = 0;
	}
	var ad_geo_ip_okrug_id_n = parseInt(getCookie("geo_ip_okrug_id"));
	if(ad_geo_ip_okrug_id_n < 0 ){
		ad_geo_ip_okrug_id_n = 0;
	}

	function get_ad_from_n(place_name) {
		if(ad_showed_from_n[place_name] === undefined){
			//adnet not select for place, selecting adnet
			var adnets = get_ad_by_ifs_n(place_name);

			adnet='none';
			if(adnets.length === 1){
				adnet = adnets[0];
			}else if(adnets.length > 1){
				adnet = adnets[getRandomInt_n(0, adnets.length-1)];
			}
			ad_showed_from_n[place_name]=adnet;
		}

		return ad_showed_from_n[place_name];
	}

	function get_ad_showed_on_n(place_name) {
		if(ad_showed_from_n[place_name] === undefined){
			return "";
		}else{
			return ad_showed_from_n[place_name];
		}
	}

	function get_localcontent_html(lc_id, max_x, max_y){
		var res_html = "";
        if(ad_local_contents_n.hasOwnProperty("contents") && ad_local_contents_n.contents.hasOwnProperty(lc_id)){
        	var local_content = ad_local_contents_n.contents[lc_id];
        	var tmpl_g_id = local_content["content_template_group_id"];
			if(ad_local_contents_n.hasOwnProperty("templates")
                && ad_local_contents_n.templates.hasOwnProperty(tmpl_g_id)
                && ad_local_contents_n.templates[tmpl_g_id].hasOwnProperty(max_x)
                && ad_local_contents_n.templates[tmpl_g_id][max_x].hasOwnProperty(max_y)
            ){
            // if(ad_local_contents_n["templates"][tmpl_g_id][max_x][max_y]["template_html"] !== undefined){
				res_html = ad_local_contents_n["templates"][tmpl_g_id][max_x][max_y]["template_html"];
				var props = ["content_rubric_title", "content_title", "content_text", "content_link", "content_image_url"];

				for (var i = 0; i < props.length; i++) {
					res_html = res_html.replace("!!"+props[i]+"!!",local_content[props[i]]);
				}
            }
        }
        return res_html;
	}

	function ad_show_lc(to_block, lc_ids, max_x, max_y){
		if(lc_ids.length === 0){
			return false;
        }
		lc_id = lc_ids[getRandomInt_n(0, lc_ids.length-1)];
		lc_html=get_localcontent_html(lc_id, max_x, max_y);

        $("#"+to_block).html(lc_html);
	}

	function get_ad_by_ifs_n(place_name) {
		var adnets=[];

		if(place_name=='d_an_l_1') {
//priority: 1
	if(( (ad_geo_ip_country_n == 'KZ'))){
		adnets.push('ar0');
	}
				if(adnets.length>0){
					return 	adnets;	
				}
				//priority: 3
	if(true){
		adnets.push('af0');
	}
				if(adnets.length>0){
					return 	adnets;	
				}
				
}
if(place_name=='d_an_l_2') {
//priority: 1

					return 	adnets;

}
if(place_name=='d_an_r_1') {
//priority: 6

}
if(place_name=='d_an_r_2') {
//priority: 4
	if(true){

	}
				if(adnets.length>0){
					return 	adnets;	
				}
				
}
if(place_name=='d_all_menu_1' || place_name=='s_all_menu_1' || place_name=='s_list_m_3_v_fix' || place_name=='s_lenta_m_2_c_fix') {
//priority: 1
	if(( (ad_geo_ip_country_n == 'KZ'))){
		adnets.push('ar0');
	}
				if(adnets.length>0){
					return 	adnets;	
				}
				
}
if(place_name=='d_rec_nat_last_v_fix' || place_name=='s_rec_nat_last_v_fix') {
//priority: 1
	if(( (ad_page_keywords_n.indexOf('ingr_471') != -1 || ad_page_keywords_n.indexOf('ingr_1500') != -1 || ad_page_keywords_n.indexOf('ingr_1474') != -1)) && ( (ad_geo_ip_country_n == 'KZ'))){
		adnets.push('ar0');
	}
if(( (ad_page_keywords_n.indexOf('ingr_651') != -1 || ad_page_keywords_n.indexOf('ingr_722') != -1 || ad_page_keywords_n.indexOf('ingr_913') != -1 || ad_page_keywords_n.indexOf('ingr_2003') != -1 || ad_page_keywords_n.indexOf('ingr_652') != -1)) && ( (ad_geo_ip_country_n == 'KZ'))){

if(( (ad_page_keywords_n.indexOf('tag_11') != -1)) && ( (ad_geo_ip_country_n == 'KZ'))){

}
if(place_name=='s_all_catf_1_v_st') {
//priority: 8

	function getRandomInt_n(min, max) {

			function getUrlContentData(url) {
				let typeId;

				var contentData = {c_type_id: 0, c_id: "", c_page: 1, utm_source: "", utm_medium:"", utm_campaign:"", utm_referrer:""};
				if(!url || !urlIsLocal(url)){
					return contentData;
				}
				var params = getUrlSearchParamsMap(url);
				var urlParced = getLocation(url);
				var urlPath = urlParced.pathname;
				var contentTypes = JSON.parse(atob('eyIxIjp7InBhdGgiOiJcL3JlY2lwZXNcL3JlY2lwZS5waHA/cmlkPSIsInBhdGhfc3RyaWN0IjpmYWxzZSwicGFyYW0iOiJyaWQiLCJuYW1lIjoicmVjaXBlcyJ9LCIyIjp7InBhdGgiOiJcL3JlYWRpbmdcL2NsYXVzZXNcLz9wb3N0X2lkPSIsInBhdGhfc3RyaWN0IjpmYWxzZSwicGFyYW0iOiJwb3N0X2lkIiwibmFtZSI6Im15YmxvZ19wb3N0cyJ9LCIzIjp7InBhdGgiOiJcL3JlY2lwZXNcL2J5dHlwZVwvP2ZpZD0iLCJwYXRoX3N0cmljdCI6ZmFsc2UsInBhcmFtIjoiZmlkIiwibmFtZSI6InRhZ3MifSwiNCI6eyJwYXRoIjoiXC9yZWNpcGVzXC9ieWluZ3JlZGllbnRcLz9paWQ9IiwicGF0aF9zdHJpY3QiOmZhbHNlLCJwYXJhbSI6ImlpZCIsIm5hbWUiOiJpbmdyaWRpZW50cyJ9LCI1Ijp7InBhdGgiOiJcL3JlY2lwZXNcL2J5aW5ncmVkaWVudFwvP2lmaWQ9IiwicGF0aF9zdHJpY3QiOmZhbHNlLCJwYXJhbSI6ImlmaWQiLCJuYW1lIjoiaW5ncmlkX2ZvbGRlcnMifSwiNiI6eyJwYXRoIjoiXC9yZWNpcGVzXC9uYXRpb25hbFwvP25pZD0iLCJwYXRoX3N0cmljdCI6ZmFsc2UsInBhcmFtIjoibmlkIiwibmFtZSI6Im5hdGlvbnMifSwiNyI6eyJwYXRoIjoiXC90aGVtZXNcLz90aGVtZV9pZD0iLCJwYXRoX3N0cmljdCI6ZmFsc2UsInBhcmFtIjoidGhlbWVfaWQiLCJuYW1lIjoidGhlbWVzIn0sIjgiOnsicGF0aCI6IlwvYmxvZ3NcLz9pZD0iLCJwYXRoX3N0cmljdCI6ZmFsc2UsInBhcmFtIjoiaWQiLCJuYW1lIjoidXNlciJ9LCI5Ijp7InBhdGgiOiJcL3Byb21vXC8iLCJwYXRoX3N0cmljdCI6ZmFsc2UsInBhcmFtIjoicHJvbW8iLCJuYW1lIjoicHJvbW8ifSwiMTAiOnsicGF0aCI6Ilwvc2VhcmNoXC8iLCJwYXRoX3N0cmljdCI6ZmFsc2UsInBhcmFtIjoic2VhcmNoIiwibmFtZSI6InNlYXJjaCJ9LCIxMSI6eyJwYXRoIjoiXC8iLCJwYXRoX3N0cmljdCI6dHJ1ZSwicGFyYW0iOiJtYWluIiwibmFtZSI6Im1haW4ifSwiOTkiOnsicGF0aCI6IlwvIiwicGF0aF9zdHJpY3QiOmZhbHNlLCJwYXJhbSI6Im90aGVyIiwibmFtZSI6Im90aGVyIn19'));

				if(params.hasOwnProperty("page")){
					contentData.c_page = params["page"];
				}
				if(params.hasOwnProperty("utm_source")){
					contentData.utm_source = params["utm_source"];
				}
				if(params.hasOwnProperty("utm_medium")){
					contentData.utm_medium = params["utm_medium"];
				}
				if(params.hasOwnProperty("utm_campaign")){
					contentData.utm_campaign = params["utm_campaign"];
				}
				if(params.hasOwnProperty("utm_referrer")){
					contentData.utm_referrer = params["utm_referrer"];
				}

				//type by params
				if(params) {
					for (typeId in contentTypes) {
						if (params.hasOwnProperty(contentTypes[typeId]["param"])) {
							contentData.c_type_id = typeId;
							contentData.c_id = params[contentTypes[typeId]["param"]];
						}
					}
				}
				//type by url
				let urlPathSub, strAfterUrl;
				if (contentData.c_type_id === 0 && urlPath && typeof urlPath == "string") {
					for (typeId in contentTypes) {
						if (typeof contentTypes[typeId].path == "string") {
							urlPathSub = contentTypes[typeId].path_strict ? urlPath : urlPath.substr(0, contentTypes[typeId].path.length);

							if (urlPathSub === contentTypes[typeId].path) {
								contentData.c_type_id = typeId;
								strAfterUrl = urlPath.substr(contentTypes[typeId]["path"].length);
								if (strAfterUrl.includes("/")) {
									contentData.c_id = strAfterUrl.substr(0, strAfterUrl.indexOf("/"))
								} else {
									contentData.c_id = strAfterUrl;
								}
								break;
							}
						}
					}
				}
				// console.log(contentData);

				return contentData;

				function getUrlSearchParamsMap(url) {
					return parseUrlSearchParamsMap(getLocation(url).search);

					function parseUrlSearchParamsMap(urlSearch) {
						var search = urlSearch.charAt(0) === '?' ? urlSearch.substring(1) : urlSearch;
						try {
							return JSON.parse('{"' + search.replace(/&/g, '","').replace(/=/g,'":"') + '"}', function(key, value) {
								return key===""?value:decodeURIComponent(value)
							});
						} catch (e) {
							return {};
						}
					}
				}
				function getLocation(url) {
					let location = document.createElement("a");
					location.href = url;
					//for IE
					if (location.host === "") {
						location.href = location.href;
					}
					return location;
				}
				function urlIsLocal(url) {
					let location = document.createElement("a");
					location.href = url;
					return (location.hostname === document.domain);
				}
			}

			function uuidv4() {
				return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function(c) {
					var r = Math.random() * 16 | 0, v = c === 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3 | 0x8);
					return v.toString(16);
				});
			}
			referrer_c = getUrlContentData(document.referrer);
			curUrl_c = getUrlContentData(window.location.href);

		<script>
			function adEvent(event, kw, ext){
				window.ib_stat_v2_events.push({event: event, in_c_type_id: 50, in_c_id: kw, event_str: ext});
			}
			var eventMethod = window.addEventListener ? "addEventListener" : "attachEvent";
			var eventer = window[eventMethod];
			var messageEvent = eventMethod == "attachEvent" ? "onmessage" : "message";

			eventer(messageEvent,function(e) {
				if(e.data.type === "ad_click"){
					console.log(e);
					adEvent("Ad Click", e.data.content, (e.data.ext !== undefined)? e.data.ext : "");
					sendAdTest("site");
					setTimeout(function() {
						sendAdTest("site7s");
					}, 7000);
				}else if(e.data.type === "ad_show"){
					console.log(e);
					adEvent("Ad Show", e.data.content, (e.data.ext !== undefined)? e.data.ext : "");
				}
			},false);

			function sendAdTest(name){
				var img = document.createElement("img");
				img.src = 'https://stat4.russianfood.com/blocks_seen/test_i.php?a='+name+'&r='+Math.round((Math.random() * 80000000) + 10000000)+'data='+encodeURI(JSON.stringify(events_module.requestData()));
				img.width = 1; img.height = 1;
				document.body.append(img);
			}

			if (document.readyState === 'complete') {
				// DOM is ready, can init now
				statInitClickEventListenersForBlock('.ya-share2');
			} else {
				// DOM loading still in progress. Init on DOM loaded
				document.addEventListener("readystatechange", function () {
					if (document.readyState === 'complete') {
						statInitClickEventListenersForBlock('.share_block');
					}
				});
			}
			function shareClick(block, service) {
				adEvent('ShareClick', service, block)
			}
		</script>

			</div>
			<script type="text/javascript">
				var scroll_pre_pixels=60;
				var nav_bar_box_id='navi_bar_box';
				var nav_bar_box_y=0;
				var nav_bar;
				var nav_bar_id='nav_bar';
				var nav_bar_el_ids=new Array('what','from','video','photo','memo','print','more','comments');
				var bar_sticky=false;
				var nav_bar_el_y=new Array();
				var nav_bar_el_y_val=new Object();

				function on_scroll_window(){
					var scroll_top=$(window).scrollTop();
					nav_bar_el_y=new Array();
					nav_bar_el_y_val=new Object();

					recalc_nav_el_y();
					nav_bar_el_y.sort(function(a,b){return a-b;});
					nav_bar_el_y.push(999999999);
					var cur_bar_el="";
					var prev_bar_x="";
					$.each(nav_bar_el_y, function(key, value) {
						if((scroll_top+scroll_pre_pixels)<value){
							cur_bar_el=nav_bar_el_y_val[prev_bar_x];
						}else{
							prev_bar_x=value
						}
					});
					$('.link-active').removeClass('link-active');
					$('#'+cur_bar_el+'_a').addClass('link-active');

					if((scroll_top>nav_bar_box_y) && (!bar_sticky)){
						nav_bar.addClass("sticky");
						nav_bar.width($("#navi_bar_box").width());
						bar_sticky=true;
					}else if ((scroll_top<=nav_bar_box_y) && (bar_sticky)){
						nav_bar.removeClass("sticky");
						bar_sticky=false;
					}
				}

				function recalc_nav_el_y(){
					$.each(nav_bar_el_ids, function(key, value) {
						var cur_el_top=$("#"+value).offset().top;
						if(value=="what"){
							cur_el_top=0;
						}
						nav_bar_el_y.push(cur_el_top);
						nav_bar_el_y_val[cur_el_top]=value;
					});
				}

				var scrollElement = 'html, body';

				function onclick_bar_el(){
					var id=$(this).parent().attr("id");
					recalc_nav_el_y();
					var scroll_to=$("#"+id.substr(0,id.length-2)).offset().top;
					$(scrollElement).stop().animate({
						'scrollTop':scroll_to-scroll_pre_pixels+15
					}, 500, 'swing');

					return false;
				}

				function show_add_to_blog(){
					$(".add_to_blog_hid").slideToggle(300);
				}

				$(document).ready(function() {
					$('html, body').each(function () {
						var initScrollTop = $(this).attr('scrollTop');
						$(this).attr('scrollTop', initScrollTop + 1);
						if ($(this).attr('scrollTop') == initScrollTop + 1) {
							scrollElement = this.nodeName.toLowerCase();
							$(this).attr('scrollTop', initScrollTop);
							return false;
						}
					});

					nav_bar=$("#"+nav_bar_id);
					nav_bar_box_y=nav_bar.offset().top;
					$(window).scroll(on_scroll_window);
					$("#nav_bar").find("a").click(onclick_bar_el);
					$(window).scroll();

					$("#add_to_blog").click(show_add_to_blog);
				});
			</script>
		</td>
	</tr>
	<tr>
		<td class="padding_l padding_r">
			<div class="sub_title_box" style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; flex-wrap:wrap;">
					<div class="sub_title_c"><h2 id="what" class="sub_title"><nobr>видео рецепт с фото пошаговый</nobr></h2></div>

	        <script>
		        var tag = document.createElement('script');

		        tag.src = "//www.youtube.com/iframe_api";
		        var firstScriptTag = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
		        firstScriptTag.parentNode.insertBefore(tag, firstScriptTag);
		        var playeryt;
		        var playeryt_is_played_send=false;
		        var playeryt_is_ended_send=false;
		        var yt_video_pixel_audit_click;
		        function onYouTubeIframeAPIReady() {
			        playeryt = new YT.Player('player0_iframe', {
				        height: '192',
				        width: '320',
				        videoId: 'og1cpJFhktU',
				        playerVars: { 'autoplay': 0},
				        events: {
					        'onReady': onYTPlayerReady,
					        'onStateChange': onYTPlayerStateChange
				        }
			        });
		        }
		        function onYTPlayerReady(event) {
			        console.info("YT load send");
			        _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Videos', 'load', 'og1cpJFhktU']);
					window.ib_stat_v2_events.push({event: 'Recipe Video Load'});
			        if(typeof yaCounter46570 !== 'undefined') {
						yaCounter46570.reachGoal('YT_load');
					}
			        video_yt_ad_audit_load();
		        }
		        function onYTPlayerStateChange(event) {
			        switch(event.data) {
				        case YT.PlayerState.ENDED:
					        YouTubeEndedSend();
					        break;
				        case YT.PlayerState.PLAYING:
					        YouTubePlayedSend();
					        break;
				        case YT.PlayerState.PAUSED:
					        if(playeryt.getCurrentTime()*100/playeryt.getDuration() > 80){
						        YouTubeEndedSend();
					        }
			        }
		        }
		        function YouTubePlayedSend() {
			        if(!playeryt_is_played_send){
				        playeryt_is_played_send=true;
				        console.info("YT playing send");
				        _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Videos', 'playing', 'og1cpJFhktU']);
						window.ib_stat_v2_events.push({event: 'Recipe Video Playing'});
						if(typeof yaCounter46570 !== 'undefined') {
							yaCounter46570.reachGoal('YT_playing');
						}
//				        ga('send', 'event', 'Videos', 'playing', '//');
				        video_yt_ad_audit_click();
			        }

		        }
		        function YouTubeEndedSend() {
			        if(!playeryt_is_ended_send){
				        playeryt_is_ended_send=true;
				        console.info("YT ended send");
				        _gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Videos', 'ending', 'og1cpJFhktU']);
						window.ib_stat_v2_events.push({event: 'Recipe Video Ending'});
						if(typeof yaCounter46570 !== 'undefined') {
							yaCounter46570.reachGoal('YT_ending');
						}
//				        ga('send', 'event', 'Videos', 'ending', '//');
			        }
		        }

		        }

		<div id="player_cont_max_width" style="width:100%"><!--&nbsp;--></div>
		<script type="text/javascript">
			function set_players_size(player_num, block_type){
				var prop=0.6;
				var max_width=704;
				var min_width=320;
				var width=min_width;
				var cont_max_width=$("#player_cont_max_width").width();

				if(cont_max_width>=max_width){
					width=max_width;
				}else if(cont_max_width<=min_width){
					width=min_width;
				}else{
					width=cont_max_width;
				}
                if(block_type=="iframe"){
                    $("#player"+player_num+"_iframe").width(width);
                    $("#player"+player_num+"_iframe").height(width*prop);
                }else{
                    $("#player"+player_num+" object").width(width);
                    $("#player"+player_num+" object").height(width*prop);
                    $("#player"+player_num+" object").attr("width",width);
                    $("#player"+player_num+" object").attr("height",width*prop);
                    $("#player"+player_num+" embed").attr("width",width);
                    $("#player"+player_num+" embed").attr("height",width*prop);
//	                $("#player"+player_num+" iframe").attr("width",width);
//	                $("#player"+player_num+" iframe").attr("height",width*prop);
	                $("#player"+player_num+" iframe").css("width",width);
	                $("#player"+player_num+" iframe").css("height",width*prop);
                }
			}

			$(document).ready(function(){
				set_players_size(0, "iframe");

			});

она должна выходить без остатков сырого теста.<br>

    </script><div class="step_n">
							<div class="img_c"><a href="https://img1.russianfood.com/dycontent/images_upl/445/big_444803.jpg" class="tozoom" target="_blank"><img src="%D0%A0%D0%B5%D1%86%D0%B5%D0%BF%D1%82%20%D0%AF%D0%B1%D0%BB%D0%BE%D1%87%D0%BD%D1%8B%D0%B9%20%D0%BF%D0%B8%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B3%20%D0%BD%D0%B0%20%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%BE%D1%80%D1%83%D1%8E%20%D1%80%D1%83%D0%BA%D1%83%20%D0%BD%D0%B0%20RussianFood_files/sm_444803.jpg" title="Фото приготовления рецепта: Яблочный пирог на скорую руку - шаг №10" alt="Фото приготовления рецепта: Яблочный пирог на скорую руку - шаг №10" border="0"></a></div>
							<p>Приятного аппетита!</p>

			<script type="text/javascript">
				$(function(){
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".thanks_text").click(thanks_send);
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".thanks").click(thanks_send);

					$(".thanks_btn").find(".no_text").click(thanks_no_click);
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".no").click(thanks_no_click);
					$(".thanks_btn").find("#no_input_send").click(thanks_no_text_send);

					$(".thanks_btn").find(".see_error").click(see_error_click);
					$(".thanks_btn").find("#see_error_input_send").click(see_error_text_send);

					//$(".res_loading").click(thanks_processed);
				});

				// thanks
				function thanks_send(){
					window.ib_stat_v2_events.push({event: 'Recipe Vote Plus'});
					vote(this,'plus','1',158159,'green','',thanks_sending,thanks_processed,thanks_no_send);
				}

				function thanks_no_click(){
					window.ib_stat_v2_events.push({event: 'Recipe Vote Minus Click'});
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".buttons").hide(200);
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".no_input").show(200);
				}

				function thanks_no_text_send(){
					let vote_text = $(".thanks_btn").find("#no_input_text").val();
					let vote_text_len_int8 = (vote_text.length < 250) ? vote_text.length : 250;
					window.ib_stat_v2_events.push({event: 'Recipe Vote Minus Send', event_int8: vote_text_len_int8});
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".no_input").hide(200);
					vote(this,'minus','1',158159,'green',vote_text,thanks_sending,thanks_processed,thanks_no_send);
				}

				function thanks_sending(){
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".buttons").hide(200);
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".res_loading").show(200);
					//window.setTimeout(function(){$(".thanks_btn").find(".td_thanks").hide(1000);},2000);
				}

				function thanks_processed(plus_minus){
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".res_loading").hide(200);
					if(plus_minus=='plus'){
						$(".thanks_btn").find(".res_you_are_welcome_text").show(200);
					}else if(plus_minus=='minus'){
						$(".thanks_btn").find(".res_thanks_text").show(200);
					}else {
						$(".thanks_btn").find(".see_error_thanks_text").show(200);
					}
				}

				function thanks_no_send(){
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".res_loading").hide(200);
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".buttons").show(200);
				}
				$(function() {
					$("#thanks_btn_buttons").hide(200);
					$("#thanks_btn_buttons").show(200);
				});
				//see_error
				function see_error_click(){
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".see_error_div").hide(200);
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".see_error_input").show(200);
					$(".thanks_btn").find("#see_error_input_text").focus();
				}

				function see_error_text_send(){
					var vote_text=$(".thanks_btn").find("#see_error_input_text").val();
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".see_error_input").hide(200);
					vote(this,'see_error','1',158159,'green',vote_text,see_error_sending,see_error_processed,see_error_no_send);
				}

				function see_error_sending(){
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".see_error_input").hide(200);
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".see_error_loading").show(200);
				}

				function see_error_processed(){
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".see_error_loading").hide(200);
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".see_error_thanks_text").show(200);
				}

				function see_error_no_send(){
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".see_error_loading").hide(200);
					$(".thanks_btn").find(".see_error_input").show(200);
				}

			</script>

			<script type="text/javascript">
	function comments_check_fields() {
					var comment_user_name = $('#comment_user_name');
			if (comment_user_name) {
				if (comment_user_name.val() == 0) {
					alert('Ошибка: напишите Ваше имя');
					comment_user_name.focus();
					return false;
				}
			}
					if ($('#comment_text').val()==0) {
			alert('Ошибка: напишите комментарий');
			$('#comment_text').focus();
			return false;
		}
		$("#comment_send_btn").val("Ожидайте...").prop('disabled', true);
		return true;
	}
</script>

						<p>У меня есть рецепт яблочного пирога, технология почти та же. 
Пирог очень хорош получается. Но там больше сливочного масла в 2 раза, 
больше сахара. У нас вообще любят положить побольше сахара, масла. Мне 
это не нравится. Поэтому обязательно на днях попробую испечь ваш пирог. 
Почти уверена, что получится очень вкусно!</p>		</div>
		<noindex>

	//,'UA'
	const cookie_policy_div = document.getElementById("cookie_policy");
	const cookie_policy_es_clist = ['A0','FR','IT','SE','PT','GR','GB','DK','DE','NL','ES','IE','BE','PL','LV','CZ','CY','HU','SK','BG','RO','AT','SI','EU','FI','EE','LT','LU','SM','MT','MC','GI','VA','HR','LI','FO','AD','GL','CS'];
	const cookie_policy_accepted = parseInt(getCookie_n("cookie_policy_accepted"));
	var cookie_policy_geo_ip_country = String(getCookie_n("geo_ip_country"));
	if(cookie_policy_geo_ip_country.length !== 2 ){
		cookie_policy_geo_ip_country = "A0";
	}
	if(isNaN(cookie_policy_accepted) && cookie_policy_es_clist.indexOf(cookie_policy_geo_ip_country) !== -1){
		cookie_policy_div.classList.add("cp_show");
	}

	function cookie_policy_accept(is_accept){
		setCookie_n("cookie_policy_accepted", is_accept, {path: "/", expires: 10 * 365 * 24 * 60 * 60});
		cookie_policy_div.classList.remove("cp_show");
	}
</script>

		adriver.prototype = { isLoading: 0, init: function(){}, loadComplete: function(){}, domReady: function(){}, onLoadComplete: function(f){var my = this; my.loadCompleteQueue.push(function(){f.call(my);}); return my;}, onDomReady: function(f){this.domReadyQueue.push(f); return this;}, reset: function(){this.loadCompleteQueue.flush(); this.domReadyQueue.flush(adriver.isDomReady); return this;} };
		adriver.extend = function(){ for(var l = arguments[0], i = 1, len = arguments.length, r, j; i<len; i++){ r = arguments[i]; for(j in r){ if(r.hasOwnProperty(j)){ if (r[j] instanceof Function){l[j] = r[j];} else if(r[j] instanceof Object){if(l[j]){adriver.extend(l[j], r[j]);}else{l[j] = adriver.extend(r[j] instanceof Array ? [] : {}, r[j]);}} else{l[j] = r[j];} } } } return l; };

ready() : setTimeout(arguments.callee, 50);})(); } else { oldOnLoad = w.onload; w.onload = function(){if(oldOnLoad){oldOnLoad();} ready();}; } }catch(e){} }, onLoadComplete: function(f){adriver.loadCompleteQueue.push(f); return adriver;}, checkLoadComplete: function(){ var i, a; for (i in adriver.items) { if (adriver.items.hasOwnProperty(i)) { a = adriver.items[i]; if (!a.prm.onScroll && typeof a.reply === 'undefined') { return false; } } } return true; }, loadComplete: function(){ if (adriver.checkLoadComplete()) { adriver.loadCompleteQueue.execute(false); } return adriver; }, setDefaults: function(o){adriver.extend(adriver.defaults, o);}, setOptions: function(o){adriver.extend(adriver.options, o);}, setPluginPath: function(o){adriver.extend(adriver.pluginPath, o);}, queue: function(flag){this.q = []; this.flag = flag ? true: false;}, Plugin: function(id){ if(this instanceof adriver.Plugin){ if(id && !adriver.plugins[id]){ this.id = id; this.q = new adriver.queue(); adriver.plugins[id] = this; } } return adriver.plugins[id]; } });
		adriver.sync = function(pair, N){ if(!adriver.syncFlag){ adriver.syncFlag = 1; var ar_duo=[];while(N--){ar_duo[N]=N+1;}ar_duo.sort(function(){return 0.5-Math.random();}); adriver.synchArray = ar_duo; } return adriver.synchArray[(!pair||pair<=0?1:pair)-1]; };
		adriver.queue.prototype = { push: function(f){this.flag ? f(): this.q.push(f);}, unshift: function(f){this.flag ? f(): this.q.unshift(f);}, execute: function(flag){var f, und; while((f=this.q.shift())){f();} if(flag == und){flag=true;} this.flag = flag ? true : false;}, flush: function(flag){this.q.length = 0; this.flag = flag ? true: false;} };
